Japanese Diet Opens, Hirota Explains Diplomatic Policy 42

Navy Insists on Equality Principle

Gradual Annexation of the Puppet State

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota delivered a speech on foreign policy at the House of Peers on the morning of the 30th, stating, "I have previously had the opportunity to present the foreign policy of the Japanese Empire at the 65th Diet. Although the cabinet has changed since then, I have continued to handle diplomatic cases according to the policies stated at that time. Subsequently, a general overview of Japan's foreign relations reveals that the understanding and recognition of the Japanese Empire's position in East Asia by the major powers has gradually increased. Consequently, relations with European and American countries, as well as the Republic of China, have also been continuously improving. This is something I find deeply gratifying. I will now report on the progress of two or three important issues in the Japanese Empire's diplomacy since the last Diet."

Naval Reduction Policy: "The naval disarmament preparatory negotiations currently being held in London, mainly involving the three major naval powers of Japan, Great Britain, and the United States, are of crucial importance. Therefore, the progress of these negotiations should be closely monitored by the Japanese Empire. The British government, seeking to facilitate the naval disarmament conference, requested that related countries hold individual preparatory negotiations in London. This occurred on May 17th of this year. The Japanese Empire government deemed the holding of the aforementioned preparatory negotiations appropriate and immediately communicated its agreement. As a result, negotiations began in London among the related countries from June 18th. Initially, opinions were exchanged regarding the procedural issues for the formal conference to be convened next year. From October, during the subsequent round of discussions, the three countries of Japan, Great Britain, and the United States engaged in negotiations on the substantive issues of disarmament. During these discussions, the Japanese Empire advocated for the consolidation of national defense, the need to maintain sufficient military strength, and the establishment of the principle of non-threat and non-aggression. Japan has consistently advocated for the rejection of the traditional ratio system and proposed establishing a common maximum limit for military strength among the related countries. Furthermore, to promote the spirit of disarmament, efforts should be made to reduce armaments, thereby alleviating the burden on the people in the future. If an agreement is to be concluded, the aforementioned common limit should be reduced as much as possible, while striving to minimize offensive military forces and enhance defensive military forces, making each country difficult to attack and easy to defend. The Japanese representatives, embodying the aforementioned policy, are working to implement their主張 and continue their efforts to conclude a rational new treaty. The Japanese Empire hopes that Great Britain, the United States, and other related countries will understand the fairness and appropriateness of Japan's主張 and that a new disarmament agreement will be established, thereby promoting world peace. This is our fervent hope. As the progress of the preparatory negotiations cannot be made public at this time, I cannot provide detailed explanations today. I will present it at a later date when an opportunity arises."

Relations with the Puppet State: "Our ally, the 'State of Manchuria,' with its spirit as an independent nation and its sound development, was solemnly proclaimed in the imperial edict when Japan withdrew from the League of Nations. This is a matter of fundamental concern for the Japanese Empire. Since then, the internal and external affairs of that country have made further progress. In March of this year, it established an imperial system, laying the foundation of the nation on a permanent basis, which is deeply gratifying. Therefore, in May of this year, His Majesty the Emperor ordered Prince Chichibu to visit Manchuria to express congratulations. As a result, the relationship between Japan and 'Manchuria' has become even closer, for which we cannot but express our deep gratitude."

Russo-Japanese Relations: "Regarding the relationship between the Japanese Empire and the Soviet Union, since my report to the last Diet, there has been a slight improvement. For example, the North Pacific fisheries have been able to conduct their business in a peaceful manner, which is a cause for celebration in the relations between the two countries. Furthermore, the negotiations for the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway, which were temporarily stalled in the early spring of this year, were resumed in March. Although encountering difficulties along the way, the Imperial government made every effort to mediate, and as a result, the total price and most of the important conditions for the transfer have been agreed upon by both parties. Currently, only three or four procedural issues remain unresolved. As these matters are complex, their resolution will require some time, but we intend to expedite the process in order to complete the negotiations."

Indo-Japanese Trade: "Next, regarding foreign trade relations, I will explain the progress of the main cases below. The trade negotiations between Japan and British India reached a general agreement on substantive issues between the representatives of both sides in February of this year. However, during the drafting of the treaty, the Indian side raised two or three important principles, causing the negotiations to stall temporarily. On April 19th, the representatives of both sides gradually engaged in informal treaty signing. Subsequently, the British and Japanese governments completed the formal signing of the Indo-Japanese Trade Treaty and its supplementary protocol. After being ratified by both sides, it came into effect on September 14th of this year. Since then, based on the actual results to date, it is known that the implementation of this treaty has been very smooth. Indo-Japanese trade has continued to develop satisfactorily on a large scale, which is a very gratifying phenomenon for both countries."

Dutch-Japanese Conference: "Finally, regarding the Dutch-Japanese conference held in Batavia, the Dutch government, faced with the economic stagnation in the Netherlands and the Dutch East Indies and in view of the sharp increase in Japanese exports to the Dutch East Indies, sought to convene a conference in January of this year to address the deficiencies of the current Dutch-Japanese trade treaty with the aim of creating a new agreement for adjustment. This was the reason for the start of the Dutch-Japanese conference. The Japanese delegation and the Dutch East Indies delegation have been discussing various issues for six months. Despite efforts to reach a compromise to conclude the conference, the issues are extremely complex and there are many obstacles. To date, the opinions of both sides have not fully aligned. However, the Japanese Empire government has consistently responded with fair and appropriate 주장. All proposals from the other party that align with the interests of both countries and have the potential for implementation have been fully considered, and we are striving for a compromise. We also hope that the conference can achieve satisfactory results in the near future, so as to enhance the friendly relations between Japan and the Netherlands."

Final Conclusion: "The above are all important cases in the recent diplomacy of the Japanese Empire. In particular, the various cases currently in progress must be brought to a satisfactory conclusion in order to mutually increase intimacy with the related countries and to make a greater contribution to the general international situation. The current internal and external situation is at a critical juncture. The implementation of our country's diplomatic policy cannot succeed without the unity of the nation and the joint cooperation of all sectors. This is what I sincerely hope for." (30th Jiji News Agency Dispatch)

Okada's Policy Speech 43

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Okada delivered a policy speech at the House of Peers today as follows:

"At this time of many difficulties and events both at home and abroad, I have humbly accepted the great responsibility of forming a cabinet. I am filled with utmost trepidation. Although I am of meager talent and strength, I will dedicate myself with sincerity and, with the cooperation of all sectors, strive to enhance the happiness of the people and manifest international justice, in order to repay the sacred trust and meet the expectations of the people. The government's policy outline was stated at the time of the cabinet's formation. From now on, we will only strive to move forward and gradually realize its implementation. Recently, disasters have occurred in various places, and many citizens are facing hardship and poverty. Therefore, relief measures need to be implemented urgently. For this reason, the government must implement effective countermeasures and further study long-term disaster countermeasures. We have included the necessary expenses in the budget and hope for your approval. Regarding rice policies, an investigation committee has been established. The government will await its response and then make efforts to proceed. Regarding the naval arms limitation conference, the government places the highest priority on ensuring national security. To establish the principle of non-threat and non-aggression among related countries and to achieve actual reduction in armaments, we aim for its realization in a fair and appropriate manner. The preparatory negotiations currently underway are being carried out by the Japanese delegation in accordance with this policy."

"Regarding the adjustment of the institutions related to 'Manchuria,' the imperial institutions prior to the Incident are insufficient to cope with the significantly changed situation after the Incident, which is beyond question. Therefore, respecting the independence of 'Manchuria,' considering the special friendly relationship between that country and Japan, and at the same time reforming the institutions in Manchuria, we aim to maintain the unity of administrative affairs related to Manchuria. The government will manage and handle all affairs related to 'Manchuria,' and its institutions have been able to avoid drastic changes, which is sufficient to address the reality of prioritizing public order work. Although there may have been some disputes in the process, which is regrettable, the fundamental purpose has been understood. Therefore, misunderstandings and unfounded fears have been completely dispelled. The budget and laws submitted this time are all urgent and cannot be delayed. We hope for prompt approval." (30th Dentsu Dispatch)

Takahashi's Financial Speech 44

(Tokyo) Finance Minister Takahashi delivered a financial speech at the House of Representatives today as follows:

"Unfortunately, this year, disasters have been frequent throughout the country. There have been floods in the Hokuriku region, droughts in Kyushu and Shikoku, and cold damage in the Tohoku region. In addition, there have been wind and flood disasters in Korea, causing great losses to local farmers. The overall damage caused by wind and flood disasters in Kansai was also very severe. As a result, the disaster has begun to affect the entire country. The exhaustion and distress of the people in the disaster-stricken areas is unbearable to witness. Furthermore, the decline in egg prices has caused great poverty in sericultural areas. In order to provide relief and recovery to these disaster-stricken areas and to implement various countermeasures, the government has allocated over 211 million yen as temporary expenses in the general account. The majority of this amount will be spent on long-term projects to recover from disasters in the 9th and 10th years of Showa. We plan to continue to spend this amount from the 11th year onwards. Therefore, the supplementary budget submitted this time for the 9th year of Showa is over 70.6 million yen, over 65.1 million yen for the 10th year of Showa, and over 75.4 million yen is planned for the 11th year of Showa and beyond. As for the content of the total amount of temporary expenses, over 116.9 million yen is allocated to the Ministry of Home Affairs for disaster civil engineering expenses, waterworks projects, etc., over 68.3 million yen is allocated to the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry for various facilities for wind and flood disasters and sericultural areas, etc., over 16.5 million yen is allocated to the Ministry of Education for the construction of primary schools in disaster-stricken areas, etc. In addition, there are over 9.4 million yen for the Ministry of Finance, the Army, the Navy, the Ministry of Justice, the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, and the Ministry of Communications for the restoration of wind and flood disasters, etc. As for relief facilities for various disasters in the general accounting sector, over 3 million yen is allocated to the special accounting capital account for communication projects, over 1.4 million yen to the business account, over 4.6 million yen to the capital account of railways, and over 10.2 million yen to the Government-General of Korea, all of which are planned to be spent from the 9th year of Showa onwards. Furthermore, the supplementary budget for the 9th year includes 38.9 million yen for the Ministry of Home Affairs, 24 million yen for the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, and 22 million yen for the Ministry of Education in relation to disasters (in units of 1,000 yen)."

"There are also over 5.6 million yen under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance, the Army, the Navy, the Ministry of Justice, and the Ministry of Communications. In addition, there are 187,000 yen for the dispatch of representatives to the Dutch-Japanese conference by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and over 60,000 yen for the facilities of the Bureau of Asian Affairs under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance. As for the financial resources, apart from over 1.08 million from ordinary revenue, the entire amount will be provided by public bonds. In the special accounting sector, regarding disaster facilities, 70 million yen is allocated to the capital account of communication projects, 1.4 million yen to the business account, 3.1 million yen to the railway capital account, and 4.3 million yen to the Government-General of Korea. The financial resources for these will come from increased revenue from communication projects, surplus from the previous year for railways, and surplus from the previous year for the Government-General of Korea, etc. In addition to the above facilities for disaster-stricken areas, there will also be reductions and exemptions of taxes and extensions of collection periods for disaster victims. In addition, the deposit banks will provide low-interest capital as much as possible to assist in reconstruction. The total amount of these loans is expected to be 200 million yen, with 96 million yen for the 9th year. It is also planned to facilitate smooth access to funds for small and medium-sized businesses through bank loans. Furthermore, the government will strive to provide relief and recovery based on the budget, but the citizens themselves should also take preventive measures to minimize the damage from natural disasters, etc., and make good use of various experiences to turn misfortune into blessing. Finally, I hope for your approval of this budget." (30th Dentsu Dispatch)

Therefore, I am not willing to ask for more detailed questions. But since it has been mentioned, the government should also feel something. Even if we do not want to force an explanation, we hope that the Prime Minister will give a reply on this point." (30th Jiji News Agency Dispatch)

British Subsidies for Shipping 46

(London) The government issued a white paper today containing an explanation of the British government's resolution to subsidize British shipping. According to the paper, the total amount of subsidies for ships on scheduled routes shall not exceed £2 million per year. If the average freight rate of such ships exceeds 92% of the freight rate in 1929 during the year the subsidy is implemented, the total amount of the subsidy may be reduced. If circumstances change during the period from January 1, 1935, to December 31, the subsidy may be canceled. The amount of advances for building new ships or renovating cargo ships shall not exceed £10 million. Advances will not be granted after two years from the passage of the necessary legislation. The white paper contains the following important changes from the one published in July: (1) For every ton of new ship built by a shipping company, two tons of old ships must be scrapped. For every ton of old ship renovated, one ton of old ships must be scrapped, which is different from the previous requirement of three tons. (2) Shipping companies may purchase British or foreign ships and scrap them. (30th Reuters Dispatch)

Opening of Japan's Great Tunnel 49

(Tokyo) The Japanese Railway Authority has been building the Enna Tunnel on the Tokaido Line for seventeen years to avoid trains climbing Mount Hakone. The tunnel was completed a few months ago at a cost of 24 million yen, with 67 workers killed. It officially opened tonight. The passage time is nine minutes, which is 20 minutes faster than the old route for express trains and one hour and 40 minutes shorter for freight trains. In addition, due to the opening of the tunnel, the timetables for all Japan, Korea, Manchuria Railway, and Chinese Eastern Railway will be uniformly revised from December 1st. (30th China United Press Dispatch)

Germany Reforming Banking Business 50

Investigative Committee Releases Report

Proposes Establishing Control Bureau to Restrict Lending

(Berlin) The German Banking Business Investigative Committee has been considering methods for reforming the banking system for a year. Over 123 experts, including Chairman Dr. Schacht, have presented their opinions. The committee released its report today, rejecting the demand for nationalizing banks. The proposed measures include seven items, which have been submitted by Dr. Schacht to German head of state Hitler for review. The seven measures are as follows: (1) Establishing a Control Bureau with full authority to control financial institutions nationwide, (2) All financial institutions and their branches must obtain official approval. The terms "bank," "banker," and "savings bank" must be legally protected. (3) There must be sufficient financial safeguards, (4) Savings bank operations must not be mixed with other banks, (5) Establishing an agency under the power of the national bank to ensure the controlled payment of loans, (6) The loan system should not be nationalized, but it should be maintained by private operators and monitored. The Control Bureau must have the power to set the maximum lending limit for each financial institution. Each financial institution must publish its report regularly, and larger institutions must publish monthly reports, (7) The Control Bureau must be well-organized to ensure the direct power of the highest national authority. Government departments must also cooperate with the Control Bureau. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

International Commercial Telegram

| Reuter's Special Commercial Telegram, December 1st |

Gold and Silver 83

London Gold Price: The London gold price today is 139 shillings and 8.5 pence, 2.5 pence higher than yesterday's price.

London Silver Bullion: In the London silver market, India was buying, and China was buying and then selling. The spot price is 24.625 pence, and the futures price is 24.75 pence. The market situation was stable at the morning close.

Exchange Rates 84

British-American: This morning, the US dollar was relatively strong in the London foreign exchange market. The opening exchange rate for British pounds to US dollars was $4.98125, which was 375 lower than yesterday's closing exchange rate for American dollars to British pounds. At noon, it fell by 4375 to $4.976875, but at 1 PM it rose by 125 to $4.978125, and this price remained unchanged until 2 PM.

British-French: In the British-French exchange market, the French franc was stable, with no change at the opening, priced at 75.53 francs. At noon, it fell by seven pounds, to 75.46 francs. This price remained unchanged until 2 PM.

Cotton and Wheat 85

American Cotton: Cotton futures opened lower due to weak market conditions in both Liverpool and Alexandria. However, spot sales were very limited, so there was a force stabilizing prices. The opening price fell by seven or eight pounds, and sentiment was quite stable afterward. Although there were sales in the South, they were absorbed by the industry.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market tended to fall because it was heard that the United States had a plan to reduce cotton production by 25% per day. At 1 PM, the January futures price was 668, down four pounds.

British Wheat: Chicago wheat futures prices fell sharply because the previous report that wheat production in Argentina was damaged was found to be false. The December futures were down 1.125 pounds, and the distant futures fell less. Grain futures also fell slightly.

Rubber 86

London: Today, the London rubber market was stable. At noon, the transaction price for January-March futures was 6.5625 pence, the same as yesterday's price.

New York: Rubber rose slightly, two or three pounds higher than the previous close, due to the stable market conditions in London. Half an hour after the opening, the market seemed to have a downward trend.

Securities 87

New York: Before the opening of the New York stock market, the factors favoring the market were: (1) This week's bank clearing was $4,177,000,000, compared with $4,084,000,000 at the same time last year, which is the first increase since mid-September; (2) There is still a continuing revival in industry and commerce; (3) Trading volume increased when prices rose. The factors unfavorable to the market were: (1) The trend of profit-taking has not weakened, and merchants are still cautious and do not readily believe in the progress of commerce; (2) The number of railway freight cars this week was 20,000 fewer than at the same time last year. The stock market opened stable this morning, with most stocks up slightly. Sentiment was still good, but after the price increase, merchants did not dare to take risks and advance. The market seemed to have a holding pattern. The prices are as follows:

Trial of the Forbidden City Treasure Theft Case Begins 94

Defamation of Character Case Awaits Summons of Defendant for Further Trial

Evidence Confirmed by Yin Qiwen, Who Testified in Court That Old Artifacts Were Stolen and Replaced

(Beijing News) The Forbidden City treasure theft case, after repeated investigations by the court and supervisory organs to collect evidence, was jointly filed on October 13th by Sun Wei, prosecutor of the Jiangning District Court, along with the bribery portion of Yi Peiji's tenure as head of the former Ministry of Agriculture and Mining. The court's criminal division began its first trial in the second criminal court yesterday (the 29th) at 10:00 AM. The defamation of character portion of the case, the plaintiff is Yin Qiwen, the defendants are Yi Peiji, Qin Hangong, Dong Lin, and Zhang Xiyin. At that time, Presiding Judge Xu Bangzhi, along with the court clerk, ascended the bench, and the court clerk summoned the parties to the court, but only the plaintiff Yin Qiwen appeared.

Defamation of Character First, Presiding Judge Xu Bangzhi declared that today's trial is investigatory in nature. Then, he asked the plaintiff his name, origin, age, and occupation. The plaintiff replied, "My surname is Yin, my given name is Qiwen, I am originally from Shaoxing, Zhejiang, residing in Beiping, 34 years old, and currently a clerk at the Forbidden City Museum." (Question) "Why are you suing Yi Peiji, Dong Lin, Qin Hangong, and Zhang Xiyin?" (Answer) "Yi Peiji colluded with Dong Lin, Qin Hangong, and Zhang Xiyin in October of last year to issue writings that damaged my reputation, and published advertisements in newspapers such as the Nanjing Xinmin Jiuguo Daily, fabricating facts and damaging my credibility and reputation." (Question) "What are the main points of the reports?" (Answer) "In the newspapers and in reports approved by the Central Supervisory Committee, the Executive Yuan, and the Judicial Administration Department, they all said that I was enticed by others, receiving monthly subsidies, and overthrowing the director in order to defame my reputation. In addition to publishing in newspapers, they also issued leaflets and pamphlets. All of these I have requested the Procuratorate of your court to investigate." At this point, the presiding judge held up the Xinmin Daily and the leaflets and pamphlets, asking if these were the items being referred to. (Answer) "Yes," and he recited the main points of the newspaper reports. Then, the presiding judge questioned why they wanted to defame his reputation. (Answer) "When Chief Prosecutor Zhu of the Supreme Court heard that Supervisory Committee members Zhou Lisheng, Gao Lu, and others had found evidence of corruption in the Forbidden City, they investigated the case. At that time, because I was one of the Forbidden City Museum staff, they asked me to inquire about the corruption situation. However, because it was my duty, I gave truthful answers, which angered Yi Peiji and others, who then colluded with Dong Lin, Qin Hangong, and Zhang Xiyin to spread writings to defame me." (Question) "Where are the defendants' addresses?" (Answer) "Yi Peiji is hiding in various cities, and his whereabouts are unknown. Qin Hangong has secretly taken his family into hiding. Dong Lin and Zhang Xiyin have been impossible to summon since leaving the Forbidden City." He also requested that the presiding judge uphold the power of the law, not only to protect personal reputation, but also to maintain the dignity of national law. The presiding judge instructed him to report the defendants' addresses to the court so that the summons and arrest warrants could be issued and the case could be prosecuted.

Evidence of Treasure Theft Then, the presiding judge asked Yin Qiwen, since he was one of the witnesses in the Forbidden City corruption case, to provide incidental testimony. Yin Qiwen, at this point, changed from the position of plaintiff to that of witness. The presiding judge then (asked) "In what part of the museum were you a clerk?" (Answer) "The Secretariat. The original Forbidden City Museum organization consisted of one department (General Affairs) and three galleries (Literature, Antiquities, and Books). When Yi Peiji became the director of the museum, in addition to the one department and three galleries, he also established the Secretariat, appointing his relative Li Zongdong as the secretary-general." (Question) "Was the director responsible for the museum affairs?" (Answer) "Because Yi Peiji was also the head of the former Ministry of Agriculture and Mining at that time, Li Zongdong handled all the powers of the Forbidden City." (Question) "What was the situation regarding corruption?" (Answer) "Some of the museum's items were sold at estimated prices, with transactions taking place every Sunday. However, Yi Peiji and Li Zongdong, not on Sundays, would authorize the appraisers at any time and purchase items at any time, which involved some corruption. Furthermore, the prices could be lowered at will. The purchasers, Yi and Li, were mainly buying furs and silks. Furs worth a total of 4,000 yuan were purchased, including more than ten pieces of sable and other furs. However, ordinary purchasers could be given a 20% discount when the value was less than 4,000 yuan. Yi and Li jointly had only 4,000 yuan, but they managed to get a 25% discount." (Question) "Where was the appraisal done?" (Answer) "Inside the museum's board of directors, priced by Li Zijiu. It was not like in a commercial place where appraisals and sales were done casually." (Question) "Is it true that the antiques were stored in the Secretariat without a responsible person to keep the keys?" (Answer) "Important boxes and cabinets were mostly in the Secretariat. The boxes and cabinets were all sealed, but the keys were indeed casually placed on the table. When Prosecutor Zhu went to investigate, he saw this situation and asked a messenger in the Secretariat, 'Are you responsible for the fact that the keys are placed on the table?' From this, it can be seen that they were opened at will." (Question) "What was the situation when the antiques were moved south?" (Answer) "The Secretariat sent people to record the items, but the items packed were randomly listed by Li Zongdong on a list. The list stated where each item was, and they were packed there without following any numbered regulations. Everything was done according to Li's orders. I asked Li what would happen when the items were checked later and the numbers did not match the check report. Li said that in this emergency situation in North China, it was like a fire, so how could we follow the numbered regulations?" (Question) "Some people say that the jewelry was unsealed after being sealed, and that the jewelry was removed from the items. What was the situation?" (Answer) "I did not handle the packing of the jewelry. I heard that after the heavy items were packed, they were placed in a specific location, waiting for the trucks to transport them south. But the jewelry, after being packed, was often moved from place A to place B, moved around at any time, without a fixed location, and often unsealed for inspection. However, the packing of the jewelry was handled by people with higher status, and at least by clerks. I was not on the scene and am not very clear." Having asked these questions, it was already 12 o'clock, and the presiding judge announced a recess and that the court would reconvene and issue summons again. (30th)

The Cause and Effect of the Assassination of King Alexander I of Yugoslavia: Lieshan 95

(Yugoslav Communication)

The Balkan Peninsula has always been regarded as the powder keg of Europe. It was not only the fuse of the last World War, which caused unprecedented catastrophe for mankind, but also the signing of the Treaty of Versailles, which had already sown the seeds of future wars. In particular, the sound of war preparations has spread throughout the world in recent years, so the actions on the Balkan Peninsula should especially attract people's attention.

The result of the World War made the contradictions between the victorious and defeated countries even more profound. In fact, the Balkan problem itself is also overly complicated. For example, religious issues, minority issues, and political issues of pro-French and pro-German factions. These problems had already become unsolvable troubles before the war. Today, this gap is even more difficult to bridge. Not only does Bulgaria feel the pain of lost land and wants to rejuvenate itself, but Hungary alone has three or four million Hungarians who are separated in Romania, Czechoslovakia, and Yugoslavia due to the lost land, becoming the most serious minority problem in the three countries. Because not only the Hungarians in the country want to restore their past prosperity, but the Hungarians abroad also feel the oppression of others and want to gain freedom and return to their motherland as soon as possible. In addition, Italy wants to intervene in the Danube River basin and the Balkan Peninsula, so it forms a system with Austria, Hungary, and Bulgaria to confront the Little Entente. This tense situation has the potential to erupt almost at any time, as long as both sides think it is necessary. Among them, the conflict between Italy and Yugoslavia is particularly intense due to the leadership of the Adriatic Sea.

Yugoslavia was Serbia before the European War. After the European War, with the help of France, it divided a part of the territory of the Austro-Hungarian Empire. On December 1, 1918, it established the Kingdom of Serbs, Croats, and Slovenes. The land area and population are about twice as large as the old Serbia. The Croats and Slovenes are of the same race as the Serbians. Before the war, the two belonged to the Austro-Hungarian Empire. After the war, under the slogan of national self-determination, they were merged into Serbia. Although everyone is of the same race, because they have been separated for too long, after the merger, the opinions of the three races have never been consistent. The so-called party struggle in the parliament is almost a struggle between the races, because everyone has their own ethnic party. On the other hand, the reason why they cannot cooperate is also related to religious beliefs. Serbians still retain the common phenomenon of Slavic people and believe in Greek Orthodox Church, while Croats and Slovenes are influenced by Rome and mostly believe in Catholicism. As a result, this situation became more and more僵, until the winter of 1928, all parties tended to extremes, and the crisis of internal change became more imminent. King Alexander I of Yugoslavia felt that this matter could not be mediated, so he dissolved the parliament by extraordinary means, amended the constitution, and re-promulgated it. In fact, he alone held great power and implemented dictatorship. At the same time, he changed the name of the Kingdom of Serbs, Croats, and Slovenes to the current name Yugoslavia (Jugoslnvian). 猶哥 means "South", originally meaning that all three races belong to the Southern Slavs, so there should be no distinction between them. As a result of the people's vote on this matter, Alexander I won and secured his power. After the failure, the opposition party, due to being oppressed, mostly fled abroad. The internal political struggle in Yugoslavia came to an end on the surface, but the opposition party was even more dissatisfied, so there was a tendency to take risks. Although Alexander I also worked hard, in principle, all ethnic groups within the borders of Yugoslavia were completely equal, regardless of each other, and in fact, it was indeed implemented, but this still could not eliminate the original estrangement. Yugoslavia is a new country and an agricultural country. Although it has also suffered from the wounds of the European War, it has gained more after the war than expected. Therefore, Yugoslavia's hope today lies in maintaining the status quo, in striving for internal construction, and not hoping for any more disturbances. Therefore, internally, it only seeks stability, and externally, it only seeks not to conflict with others. Yugoslavia would be satisfied. However, the neighboring countries have the opposite view. The Italians are ambitious and want to develop outwards and restore the prestige of the old Roman Empire. The Hungarians are gnashing their teeth at their lost land, and they are indeed licking their wounds and waiting for the opportunity. The Bulgarians are always thinking about their lost territory. This means that Yugoslavia is in a situation of being surrounded on three sides. After the treaty between Italy and Albania was signed, Italy's power extended to the southern border of Yugoslavia. In short, Yugoslavia is in a situation of being surrounded on four sides.

Under this situation, it is natural to be disappointed to talk about peace. Therefore, Yugoslavia signed a military alliance treaty with France in 1927, and further contacted Romania and Czechoslovakia to form the Little Entente, in case of emergency. However, in the end, due to the ambition of the Italians, Yugoslavia always felt uneasy and tried its best to break through the Italian encirclement plan. Therefore, in 1933, King Alexander I of Yugoslavia personally traveled to the Balkan Peninsula for the first time, wandering through Romania, Turkey, Greece, and other countries. After returning home, he signed a Balkan treaty with various countries. Because the Bulgarians always failed to understand Yugoslavia, in October of this year, Alexander I personally went to Bulgaria to discuss cooperation between the two sides. According to reports from all parties, the result of this trip was very good. If this is the case, Yugoslavia can be free from worries about the East in case of war.

After Alexander I returned to Yugoslavia from Bulgaria, he took a warship to France. The most important mission of his trip was naturally the issue between Italy and Yugoslavia. Because France's fear of Germany has increased year by year, it wants to compromise with Italy as much as possible, and the rapprochement between France and Italy must first resolve the contradiction between Italy and Yugoslavia. Therefore, this trip by Alexander I is of great importance to the future of Yugoslavia. But unfortunately, when he arrived in Marseille, he was assassinated less than ten minutes after landing. French Foreign Minister Barthou, who was welcoming him, was also killed in the same car. The murderer was a Bulgarian, a member of the Bulgarian assassination group. However, according to opinions from all parties, this assassination case has nothing to do with Bulgaria, and the most suspected are Italy and Hungary.

According to news from Yugoslav political circles, for many years, Yugoslavia's opposition party members have been used in Italy and Hungary to organize a別働隊, who often enter and leave Yugoslav territory, assassinate important political figures, and prepare for riots. It is said that many times have been uncovered, and the murderer has also confessed various inside stories. This time, the group of murderers entered France from Hungary via Switzerland with fake Czech passports. The weapon used by the murderer was a latest type of machine gun pistol, which belonged to military weapons. Because there is no manufacturer's name on it, if it is not supplied by a national military agency, the murderer cannot buy this weapon alone. Naturally, the details are very bizarre.

Since King Alexander I of Yugoslavia was assassinated, the situation in the Balkans has suddenly shown a very tense situation, and war is almost in danger of breaking out at any time. However, after all, all parties are not fully prepared, and everyone has not yet taken advantage of this opportunity to act. At this time, what is being argued is nothing more than the issue of moral responsibility. The Little Entente held a meeting in Belgrade, the capital of Yugoslavia, to push the entire responsibility for this incident onto Italy and Hungary. Then Italy and Hungary will show weakness in world opinion. Conversely, Italy, Hungary, and other countries are trying their best to recognize this incident as an internal political assassination case in Yugoslavia, which has nothing to do with other countries. Everyone is currently fighting a big pen war in this regard. The danger of war has been temporarily avoided. Although, the fundamental conflict not only still exists, but after this incident, it has a tendency to expand further.

After the death of the King of Yugoslavia, the internal affairs of Yugoslavia are temporarily not affected by any major impact. The internal and external policies will probably still follow his past political path. The throne is now inherited by Prince Peter, known as Peter II. Peter II is currently eleven years old, and the power is jointly responsible by three regents until Peter II reaches the age of eighteen. The three regents are Prince Paul, former Minister of Education Stan Koyevic and Dr. Borovkovic.

The coffin of the King of Yugoslavia was transported back from Marseille by the Yugoslav warship. The funeral was held in the capital Belgrade on October 18. On that day, hundreds of thousands of people came from all over the country, especially the farmers of Serbia, whose mourning was touching. Originally, Serbia had been under the rule of Turkey for a long time. The ancestors of Alexander I were originally wealthy farmers of the Serbian race who had gathered people to fight against the Turks. Later, with the help of Imperial Russia, they were able to break away from Turkey and establish a marquisate. The ancestors of Alexander I also gained the throne because of this. Therefore, the relationship between the Yugoslav royal family and the farmers is very different from other countries. This time, the death of Alexander I made the mourning of the Serbian farmers even more悲切, because Yugoslavia has today, from the status of an oppressed nation, striving to become an independent country with a population of 14 million. In the simple minds of ordinary farmers, all of this is the credit of King Alexander I of Yugoslavia.

Alexander I was born on December 17, 1888, and was the fourth son of the late King Peter I. He studied in Geneva in his early years, and later studied the army in Petrograd, the old Russian capital. In 1909, after his elder brother Prince George voluntarily inherited the throne, Alexander I was formally considered the heir. In the Balkan War against the Turks in 1912, he served as the commander-in-chief. His military exploits made him an idol of the general public. When the World War broke out in 1914, Peter I handed over all power to Alexander I to manage, especially the military, which was almost entirely commanded by him alone. On August 16, 1921, after his father passed away, he formally inherited the throne. On June 8, 1922, he married Princess Maria of Romania, and had three sons, namely the current King of Yugoslavia Peter II, Prince Tomislav, who is currently six years old, and Prince Andrew, who is currently five years old. In short, the Yugoslav royal family has a relatively stable foundation in the country, so although in this era of trends, and after Alexander I was assassinated, it is still able to maintain the status quo, which is not an easy thing. The future situation will probably still depend on the development of the Italy-Yugoslavia incident. Because Yugoslavia is an agricultural country with no serious unemployment problem, since the drought has spread all over the world this year, the prices of agricultural products have risen a lot, which has given Yugoslavia a lot of economic help. Therefore, the people of Yugoslavia are bound to be poor, but they are able to support a family. Their food and housing problems can barely be solved. What they lack is only cash. Compared with industrial countries, it is slightly better.

and French Foreign Minister Barthou (right)

Shanghai South Railway Station Scheduled Air Defense Drill 119

The Shanghai South Railway Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway will hold a major air defense drill on December 4th. The scenario assumes that at 3:30 AM, six enemy bombers will fly from the east towards Shanghai at an altitude of approximately 2,500 meters and a speed of 280 kilometers per hour. At 3:35 AM, they will drop several incendiary bombs on the Shanghai South Railway Station. The railway's South Station police will conduct a security and alert drill against the enemy, involving: (1) Alarm, (2) Security alert, (3) Blackout, (4) Emergency alarm, (5) Rescue dispatch, (6) Emergency response dispatch, (7) Firefighting dispatch, (8) Alarm lifted, (9) Each team returns to its original position, (10) Air defense command of both railways makes comments, (11) Drill completed. (Alarm symbols) (1) The alarm bell will sound one long ring and two short rings, continuously for eight times. (2) The emergency alarm bell will sound continuous rapid strikes. (3) The alarm cancellation bell will sound slow strikes six times, continuously for eight times. (4) The existing bell at the station will be used as the alarm bell. (Drill procedure) (1) The Engineering Department will pile up burning firewood. (2) Sound the alarm bell. (3) Each team assembles at the designated work location and simultaneously goes on alert. (4) Issue an emergency alarm and turn off the lights. (5) Incendiary bombs ignite. (6) The fire brigade is dispatched. (7) The rescue team is dispatched. (8) The ambulance is dispatched (directly from the locomotive shed to the platform). (9) Mock thugs invade from the front of the South Station. (10) The alarm is lifted and the lights are turned on.

Liu Xiang and He Chengjun Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday 120

Liu Talks – Consulted with Chiang on Methods to Suppress Communist Bandits in Sichuan

He Talks – Disaster Victims Everywhere in Hubei Province, Relief Efforts Underway

According to the Central News Agency, Liu Xiang, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression and Reconstruction in Sichuan, and He Chengjun, Pacification Commissioner of Hubei Province, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 7:20 AM on the overnight express train from Nanjing. Liu came to have his health checked and treat his diabetes, as well as to visit the site of the January 28th Incident in Shanghai. He accompanied Liu on his trip to Shanghai to visit friends in the Shanghai area, and plans to stay for about three or four days. The details of their arrival in Shanghai are as follows:

Liu and He Arrive in Shanghai 121

After Liu paid his respects to Chairman Chiang in Nanjing, he originally planned to return to Sichuan immediately to handle military affairs related to the suppression of bandits in Sichuan. However, due to years of handling military affairs, he felt physically exhausted, and his diabetes recurred. He took the opportunity to come to Shanghai to have his health checked. His arrival in Shanghai was rushed, so few people knew about it. Only Yang Hu, Director of the Municipal Security Bureau, and Secretary Wang Zhijing, and others welcomed him at the station. The Municipal Security Bureau also sent a company of security guards to the station to provide security. Liu and He got off the train amidst the welcoming cheers and went to their hotel to rest.

Liu Undergoes Health Examination 122

Those who accompanied Liu to Shanghai included Secretary-General Zhang Bigou, Liu's representative in Hankou Qiu Jia, his representative in Shanghai Deng Mingjie, two adjutants, and bodyguards, a total of eight people. After arriving at the hotel, he immediately invited physician Lü Shoubai to examine his health. Then, at his residence, he telegraphed his old friends in Shanghai to meet. At 9:00 AM, he went to Baolong Hospital on Baker Road to have his health checked and treat his diabetes, returning to his residence around 12:00 PM. In the afternoon, Liu went to the city center to visit Mayor Wu and visit various construction projects. He then went to the Wusong forts and other areas of the January 28th Incident to visit the war zone. He visited Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, yesterday afternoon around 5:30 PM, talking for about half an hour before leaving. Yang Hu, Director of the Municipal Security Bureau, hosted a banquet for Liu and He at his private residence on Huanlong Road yesterday at noon, and the guests and hosts enjoyed themselves until around 2:00 PM before dispersing.

Liu's Remarks 123

Liu was wearing a gray suit, a thick black wool coat, and glasses on his nose. He was tall and thin, with gray hair. According to Liu, he took the opportunity of his trip to Nanjing to visit Shanghai to treat his diabetes. He will stay in Shanghai for about three days before returning to Nanjing to pay his respects to Chairman Chiang again. He plans to leave Nanjing for Sichuan in a week. The military situation for suppressing the bandits in Sichuan is currently not advancing. He had already consulted with Chairman Chiang in Nanjing on methods of suppression. As soon as he returns to Sichuan, he will order a general attack. The bandits are currently occupying the Tongjiang-Wanyuan county area, with about 60,000 to 70,000 people and 20,000 to 30,000 firearms, making it necessary to mobilize 100,000 troops to encircle and suppress them. Sichuan's finances can usually balance revenue and expenditure, but due to the ongoing period of bandit suppression, military expenses are numerous, resulting in a shortfall. He has also consulted with Finance Minister Kong in Nanjing and a method has been agreed upon: the Ministry of Finance will send personnel to Sichuan to jointly reorganize national taxes. The rumor that Sichuan is issuing public bonds of 70 million yuan is a misunderstanding. As for transporting 10 million taels of silver to Sichuan, it is because Sichuan lacks silver to regulate finance. Regarding construction in Sichuan, there are many plans, but they cannot be carried out due to the ongoing bandit suppression. The important ones include building the Chengdu-Chongqing Railway and developing sugar production and salt fields. Once the communist bandits are eliminated, we will actively carry them out.

[Caption under a picture of Liu Xiang with a hat:] Liu Xiang (holding a hat) poses for a photo in front of the Municipal Government

He's Remarks 124

According to He Chengjun, he came to Shanghai to visit friends and will return to Nanjing within three or four days to attend the Fifth Plenary Session on December 10th. Zhang Xueliang has already entered Nanjing from Hubei to attend the meeting. As for the banditry in Hubei Province, after vigorous suppression, the bandit gangs have dispersed. The banditry in the entire province will soon be resolved. However, after being disturbed by bandits, disaster victims are everywhere and many are homeless. The provincial government is currently conducting relief efforts.

Sanbei Company's Taishan Ship Encountered Wind En Route, Did Not Arrive 125

Company Sends Telegram to Inquire

No Definite News

The Sanbei Company's Taishan ship departed from Qingdao on November 27th. On the 29th, the Shanghai company did not receive a telegram from the ship. The company was very concerned. Because direct telegram calls went unanswered, they telegraphed the Qingdao branch to inquire about its whereabouts. They subsequently received a reply stating that the Taishan had fully loaded coal and departed from Qingdao, heading for Shanghai. There has been no news since then. This newspaper had already learned about this matter on Thursday afternoon. However, because the company still found it difficult to confirm the facts, it was not disclosed in the newspaper. However, there was indeed a strong wind on the sea on the night of the 27th. Yesterday morning, there was a message stating that the Taishan ship had temporarily stopped to avoid the wind in the Xiaoshanji Bay, 120 nautical miles from Qingdao, and its radio had been destroyed by wind and waves, so it could not report. The reporter went to the company to inquire about the truth. According to people in the company, when the Taishan left Qingdao for Shanghai, the Yutai Xing, another ship in Shanghai, also left Qingdao. They encountered a strong wind en route. Now that the ship has arrived in Shanghai, there is no doubt that the Taishan encountered wind. However, it is widely rumored that the Taishan may have had an accident. Because the matter was serious, the reporter again inquired with the person in charge of the Sanbei Company about the news of the Taishan ship. According to reports, no telegrams had been received in Shanghai since the Taishan left Qingdao, and Shanghai's calls went unanswered. Whether it had an accident or not, the company had not received a factual report to prove it and could not say for sure but was still trying to find out. It is understood that the Taishan ship has a deadweight of 2,261 tons and a net tonnage of 1,420 tons. It was built in 1906. This year, in order to open the Nanhua route, it underwent major repairs in the dock and was thoroughly rebuilt, with passenger seats installed. This time, it was loading coal in Qingdao to come to Shanghai.

Japanese Newspaper Reports HSBC Bringing Back Cash 132

To Ease Financial Panic

Yesterday's Japanese Daily News reported that the panic in the financial world is expanding, with the decline of public bonds and stocks and the rise of cotton, silk, and cotton, resulting in fluctuations in the value of currency. As a result, the credit of paper money and cash is gradually diverging. The state of anxiety in the financial world is imminent. The Ministry of Finance and financial operators are doing their best to reverse the crisis. Among them, the negotiation with HSBC to re-import cash from Hong Kong may alleviate the current financial situation. However, HSBC has agreed in principle to the re-import of silver, but on the condition that if it is re-exported in the future, it will be tax-free. The Ministry of Finance believes that China has not yet escaped from the silver standard and does not agree to this condition. It is said that HSBC may not object on the surface.

Recent Situation of the Yellow River Blocking Project 134

The Yellow River Water Disaster Relief and Work Relief Group has been diligently supervising and expediting the Yellow River blocking project at Changyuan. The group received telegrams yesterday from Liu Bingzhong and Sang Ze, inspectors dispatched by the Bian Office, as well as Hua Deming, Director of the Hebei River Affairs Bureau, stating that after the continuous work on guiding levees at Guantai, the river flow has become smoother. As of the 26th, at Longmenkou, the constructed sections include a 53-zhang (approx. 177 meters) long levee at the west station, an 11-zhang (approx. 37 meters) long earthen dam at the east station, and a 14-zhang (approx. 47 meters) long revetment levee. The current water depth is 3.2 meters. Due to the rainy and windy weather today, the water conditions are unstable. The Bian Office sent a telegram instructing that the blocking work be strictly expedited after the weather clears to avoid delays. A reply telegram received later on the 27th indicated that work was still being intensified, with the west dam being extended by 2.5 zhang (approx. 8.3 meters) and the east dam having a 14-zhang (approx. 47 meters) revetment levee added. With such rigorous supervision, it is expected that the river will be blocked and the flow cut off soon. Furthermore, the Yellow River Blocking Project Fund Management Committee, jointly established by the group, the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, and the Hebei Provincial Government, has been working intensely in Bian since its establishment. The central government's allocated subsidy of 100,000 yuan has already been remitted and stored for safekeeping. However, since the Hebei Province's allocated funds have not yet arrived, Director Kong Xiangrong telegraphed Minister Kong, who in turn telegraphed the Chairman, urging the full allocation of 100,000 yuan as per the original plan, to match the central government's approved 200,000 yuan for the blocking project. Yesterday, a report from the Bian Office indicated that the 100,000 yuan to be allocated by Hebei Province has also been remitted in full, ensuring that the funds are ready and awaiting allocation for construction use. For this Yellow River blocking project, the Guantai Jiugu Road and Da Niezhuang projects are being undertaken simultaneously. Due to the urgency and difficulty of the project, the original budget estimated by the Hebei River Affairs Bureau was over 300,000 yuan. Following approved procedures, the group, together with the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, thoroughly discussed and approved a revised budget of over 197,000 yuan, with detailed explanations provided. However, Director Kong believes that the more shoreline protection that can be done, the more protective force it will provide. He is scheduled to come to Beijing to discuss specific measures with Minister Kong, whereby the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association will issue a letter to Director Kong, who will travel to Henan Province within days to negotiate with the Henan authorities regarding the small water interception dam project within the embankment, previously built by the China International Famine Relief Commission and now damaged. He will request that the Henan Provincial Government allocate funds for its repair, as the completion of this dam is highly beneficial to the local people of Henan. The Henan provincial authorities had originally expressed their willingness to assist, and it is likely that this will become a reality. Moreover, fearing that the cold weather might make it difficult to extract soil and hinder the blocking project, Director Kong inquired about the weather conditions at the construction site during his recent trip to Beijing, which coincided with rainy and windy weather in the city and a drop in temperature. He received a reply telegram from the Bian Office stating that the weather had cleared on the 27th, with the temperature at 48 degrees (Fahrenheit), and 50 degrees (Fahrenheit) on the 28th, with regular inspections being conducted at the site and daily reports being submitted.

Special Commissioner Zhang Wuyuan of Henan Province Leaves Shanghai 136

Mr. Zhang Wuyuan, the special commissioner for statistical investigation dispatched by the Henan Provincial Government, came south to investigate statistical affairs. Mr. Zhang and his party completed their official business on the 30th and returned north. According to Mr. Zhang, he was originally ordered to investigate in Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Shanghai, and Hangzhou, but due to the time constraint, he regrettably could not visit Hangzhou. Regarding the three places visited, he gained very positive impressions. The statistics departments of the Central Party Headquarters in Nanjing, the National Government's Bureau of Statistics, the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Shanghai Municipal Council of the British and French Concessions can be considered models. With the advancement of science, the effectiveness of statistics is extensive, and its importance is profound. Therefore, strict attention must be paid to the organization's structure, the precision of charts, and the accuracy of numbers, as even the slightest error can lead to significant inaccuracies. The statistics produced by the aforementioned departments have excellent results in all the above aspects. In particular, the authorities of the British and French Concessions employ the latest European and American methods and various statistical instruments, which are worthy of reference for Chinese people. Taking the statistical analysis machine as an example, even with extremely complex occupational statistics, classification using this machine can yield accurate results in the shortest possible time. Other examples can be inferred from this. During his trip south, Mr. Zhang visited various places and learned from others' strengths to correct his own weaknesses, gaining a lot of benefits. After returning to Henan, he will organize and refine the materials collected during this trip, improve the Henan statistical plan, and submit it to the Provincial Chairman for adoption and implementation. He only provided a brief overview based on what he saw and heard and did not dare to make any presumptuous criticisms. He also expressed his gratitude for the sincere hospitality of the municipal government, the concession authorities, and other organizations in this city.

Mrs. Yen Fu-ching's Spirit of Sacrifice 137

Precious Blood Transfused to Patient

Since President Yen took over the First Hospital of the Chinese Red Cross Society, he has hired experts and established specialized departments, and the medical services have been improving daily. Recently, a maternity patient, Mrs. Huang Xu, suffered severely from uterine cancer. After examination, it was determined that a blood transfusion was necessary for any hope of recovery. However, a blood transfusion is related to the health of the blood donor, and it was difficult to find a suitable person for a while. After several discussions, no solution was reached. Mrs. Yen Fu-ching happened to hear about this and believed that doctors should have the spirit of "cutting off a piece of flesh to cure the patient." If it could cure the disease, she was willing to donate her own precious blood to the patient. She went to the hospital and asked the doctors to perform the blood transfusion procedure, which went very well. This spirit of acting bravely for a just cause is truly commendable, and it reflects the spirit of diagnosis and treatment in the hospital.

Situation of the Changzhou Farmers Bank Handling Cattle Mortgage Loans 139

The Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank, recognizing that the farmers in the disaster-stricken areas of various counties this year are suffering greatly and will inevitably be forced to sell their livestock, drafted measures for cattle loans in order to prevent this from affecting the spring plowing in the coming year. This draft was submitted to the Supervisory Committee for approval and distributed to various branch offices for reference. It has been learned that the Changzhou, Yixing, and other branches have already implemented these measures, and the requests for loans have been very enthusiastic. In Changzhou alone, over 4,000 cattle have been mortgaged, and there are still many applications being received. Cattle mortgage loans in Wuyi County are handled separately at the warehouses in Benniu, Buyiqiao, Dong'an, and Nanshuxia. The mortgaged cattle are branded on their horns but are still returned to the farmers for plowing. The county government issued a notice stating that the cattle cannot be bought or sold before the mortgage is cleared. A guarantee is provided by three or more neighbors, certified by the township office, and a reliable shop is found to guarantee repayment responsibility.

Dr. Mei Guozhen, American Medical Doctor, Opens Practice Today 140

Dr. Mei Guozhen is the nephew of Dr. Shi Meiyu, President of the Bethel Hospital in this port, and the son of Mei Shiyunying, President of the Chinese Christian Fuyu Industrial Children's Home. He was a bright student at Shanghai University in his youth. In 1926, he studied political science at Johns Hopkins University in the United States. He was intelligent and hardworking, ranked at the top of his class, and was admitted to the university's excellent society. In 1928, he transferred to medicine, studied diligently, and delved into the depths of modern medical technology. After graduating in medicine in 1933, he interned at St. Lukce's Hospital and Bethlehem Hospital, where he quickly became famous for his steady and rapid surgery skills. As a result, an American female physician, Wilma Stiles, admired him and eventually married him. Dr. Mei is not only skilled in medicine, but he also held various important positions in Chinese student organizations in the United States. He represented China at the International Youth Conference as the president of the Chinese Student Christian Association in the United States. His enthusiastic service is evident. His skills in lecturing, music, and social interaction are also worth mentioning. This summer, Dr. Mei and his wife and son returned to their homeland. He was hired by the Bethel Hospital and performed a caesarean section on a difficult birth, saving both mother and child. He is scheduled to officially open his practice on December 1st. Dr. Mei's skills are a cause for celebration for the future of Chinese medicine.

Sanders, Director of the Shaoguan Puguang Orphanage, Comes to Beijing and Shanghai to Raise Funds 141

Donated 25,000 Yuan

The Child Welfare Association Hosts a Banquet in Appreciation

The American philanthropist Sanders, 65 years old, came to China during the late Qing Dynasty and has served for over thirty years. In the thirteenth year of the Republic (1924), with the consent and assistance of the late Premier and Madam Soong Ching Ling, he established the Puguang Orphanage in Shaoguan, Guangdong, to carry out the work of rescuing children. Initially, the scale was very small, but later, through continuous efforts, he expanded the site to over 400 mu (approx. 26.7 hectares) and built twelve buildings of various sizes. In addition to primary and secondary school courses, there are also planting, animal husbandry, dyeing, and other workshops. There are currently fifteen teachers, doctors, and nannies, as well as over 200 orphans. The results are quite excellent. Recently, the director, seeking greater development, traveled north to Beijing and Shanghai with Zeng Jiucheng, a staff member of the orphanage, to visit Chairman Lin of the National Government, Premier Wang, Sun Ke, Kong Xiangxi, Wang Zhengting, Mayor Wu of Shanghai, and other important figures. They received donations of 25,000 yuan and hired Zhu Ziqiao, Wang Yiting, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Qu Wenliu, Feng Yangshan, Huang Hanzhi, Zhao Jinqing, Guan Jiongzhi, and others as honorary directors of the orphanage. The results of the meetings were very satisfactory. The Shanghai Child Welfare Association believes that Sanders, as a foreigner, has shown such enthusiasm for China's child welfare cause, which is rare and commendable. Therefore, it hosted a banquet at the Da Zhonghua Restaurant on Sichuan Road yesterday at noon to show its appreciation. In addition to Sanders and Zeng Jiucheng, those present included Chen Tiesheng, Deputy Director-General of the Child Welfare Association, Chen Zhengfan, Zhao Jian, and Quan Shaowen, a member of the Beijing Child Welfare Association. They had a pleasant conversation and took a group photo as a souvenir. It is reported that Director Sanders, encouraged by the success of this trip, is scheduled to take the French postal ship Athos at 10:00 this morning, returning to Guangdong and then to Shaoguan.

A Policeman Steals a Leather Belt and is Apprehended 143

The Truth Comes to Light After Discovery

The Policeman is Sentenced to One Year and Two Months in Prison

Tang Qinggui, a worker at the Zhongfu Silk Mill on Hengfeng Road in Zhabei, stole several leather belts worth 300 yuan from the factory at around 5:00 AM on November 25th, intending to take them to the concession to sell them for money. However, he was stopped at the south end of the Wuzhen Road Bridge by Wang Zhiliang, a Chinese policeman No. 2347, and Cai Kunshan, a Chinese policeman No. 390, both stationed at the bridge by the Xinzha Police Station. Seeing Tang acting suspiciously, they arrested him and interrogated him. Tang initially denied it but then confessed that he had stolen them from the Zhongfu Silk Mill and begged for leniency. The two policemen, thinking that no one knew about this matter, had the idea of pocketing the items. They confiscated the leather belts and let Tang go. Tang also thought that he had escaped from the jaws of death, which was a great fortune, so he went back to the factory, preparing to continue working. Unexpectedly, the factory owner, Han Songwen, suspected that Tang had stolen something and reported it to the Public Security Bureau, who sent a detective to arrest and interrogate Tang. Tang knew that there was nothing to hide, so he told the truth. The bureau chief, after verifying the confession, immediately took Tang Qinggui to the Xinzha Police Station to state their intention. The police chief gathered all the Chinese policemen in the station and asked Tang to identify them. Tang immediately identified Wang Zhiliang, policeman No. 2547, and said that there was another policeman who was not present today. The police chief detained policeman Wang and investigated whether policeman Wang was indeed on duty with policeman Cai Kunshan, No. 390, on the night shift at the Wuzhen Road Bridge. However, Cai had not come to the station for roll call and had fled after learning of the situation. All the stolen goods, the leather belts, had also been taken away by policeman Cai. Therefore, policeman Wang was escorted to the First Special Court by the police station on the morning of the 28th, requesting temporary detention for investigation. In addition to denying any collusion in court, the lawyer, Fan Gang, applied for bail for him. Judge Wu ordered Wang Zhiliang to be released on bail, subject to being summoned at any time, with a shop as his guarantor, pending investigation. Yesterday morning, the date for the trial arrived, and Wang also surrendered to the court to await questioning. According to the police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, who stated the case, during the detention period, the police station determined that policeman Wang's previous statement was completely false, and he was in collusion with Cai, who was at large. Therefore, he was formally prosecuted in accordance with Article 172 of the Criminal Law for facilitating escape and Article 376 for receiving stolen goods, and requested a strict investigation. Furthermore, according to the confession of the suspect, Tang Guangui, obtained by the Public Security Bureau, he was stopped by Chinese policeman No. 390 while passing the south end of the Wuzhen Road Bridge that morning, and the leather belts were confiscated. He was released after begging, but Wang was also present at the time and soon left for another place. When questioned, the defendant still equivocated and tried to deny his guilt. After verifying the confession, Judge Wu Tingqi sentenced Wang Zhiliang to one year and two months in prison for jointly facilitating escape. The number of days of detention before the final judgment will be counted at two days for each day of imprisonment. Wang Zhiliang was taken into custody, and Tang Qinggui was taken back by the Public Security Bureau for questioning.

The Late Owner of Hua Rongchang Candle Shop's Wives and Concubines Dispute the Inheritance, Leading to Litigation 144

Differences of Opinion Between the Parties Make Mediation Impossible

Next to the Hong Temple (i.e., the Bao'an Situ Temple) on Nanjing Road, there are two incense and candle shops, one is Hua Rongchang and the other is Wangchang. The business of these two shops relies entirely on the temple, as the temple's incense is perpetually flourishing. Especially during the new moon and full moon of the lunar calendar, superstitious women flock to the temple, and customers also throng to these two shops, wearing out their thresholds. The owners of both shops have become wealthy. The owner of Hua Rongchang was from Ningbo. In the past, his wife and concubine had litigated in the former Mixed Court over the management of the shop. The owner of Wangchang, Mr. Huang, was also from Ningbo. He had been in the incense and candle business for many years. In addition to the shop next to the Hong Temple, he also had several branch shops. His family was very wealthy. Mr. Huang originally had one wife and one concubine. The wife was named Hua Caiqin. Although the concubine had no children, she had raised a son named Hanqing in his early years, who is now only fifteen years old. Unexpectedly, Mr. Huang died of illness on September 16th of this year. The huge amount of property he left behind was entirely controlled by Hua Caiqin. The concubine is now only thirty-seven years old. Fearing that it would be difficult for the mother and son to maintain their livelihood in the future, she asked the main wife to divide the inheritance. However, Hua Caiqin sternly refused. Although relatives were invited to mediate, it was to no avail. The concubine then, in the name of her adopted son's legal guardian, retained a lawyer to submit a petition to the Civil Mediation Office of the First Special District District Court, requesting mediation. However, after the mediation court investigated the matter, it was determined that the claims of the two parties were irreconcilable and a peaceful resolution was impossible. Therefore, the concubine formally sued Hua Caiqin, requesting a judgment ordering the defendant to hand over all the inheritance for legal division. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qiao Wanxuan of the Civil Division of the First Special District Court held a hearing. The defendant failed to appear in court. The plaintiff's attorney briefly stated the grounds for the lawsuit. Judge Qiao then adjourned the hearing to 2:00 PM on October 6th, ordering the defendant to appear in court for further interrogation.

Exhibition of Improved Chinese Bookkeeping to Open Today 150

Lecture Meeting to Be Held Tomorrow Morning

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce will hold an exhibition of improved Chinese bookkeeping for three days starting today. The lecture notes, books, accounts, forms, and practical achievements used in the lecture courses will be displayed publicly. Tomorrow (i.e., the 2nd) morning, a lecture meeting will be held, with prominent figures from the business community attending to give speeches. The details are continued below:

Display List The exhibition site is located in the regular meeting room and reception room on the second floor of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. The arrangement of the exhibits has been completed by personnel from the Xu Certified Public Accountant Office. The exhibits include more than 40 types of Xu's improved Chinese account books and forms, totaling more than 200 books. There are also various practical account styles from the lecture courses, divided into six organizations, also totaling more than 200 books. In addition, there are various books and magazines on improved Chinese bookkeeping on display. Charts, explanations, and inscriptions by celebrities are hung on the walls. It is reported that various printed materials and samples will be distributed today.

Joint Notice The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Commercial School, and the Xu Yongzuo Accounting Tutorial School have jointly issued a notice for the achievement exhibition of the improved Chinese bookkeeping lecture course, which reads: (1) The first class of students in the improved Chinese bookkeeping lecture course jointly organized by our schools has now graduated. The daily curriculum focuses on practical exercises in improved Chinese account books and forms. The achievements of each item can be used as a reference for those who are interested in improving bookkeeping. It is scheduled to be held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce from December 1st to 3rd, from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM every day. At the same time, the latest revised improved Chinese bookkeeping lecture notes, account styles, books, charts, and various account books and forms recently published by the Standard Account Form Document Production Office will be displayed together for comparison. We respectfully hope that people from all walks of life will come to guide and teach. (2) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to the industrial and commercial associations, stating: We are writing to inform you that, in view of the importance of improving Chinese bookkeeping, our affiliated commercial night school and Xu Yongzuo Certified Public Accountant have jointly established an improved Chinese bookkeeping lecture course to teach the principles and methods of improving Chinese bookkeeping. We have previously sent a letter to your association, notifying all members to recommend students for registration. Now that the lecture course has ended, we have decided to publicly display various achievements in the regular meeting room of our association on December 1st, 2nd, and 3rd. A variety of newly released improved Chinese account books and forms will also be displayed together. Each student will be responsible for explaining them. On the morning of the 2nd, at 10:00 AM, Xu Yongzuo Certified Public Accountant and prominent figures from the business community will give speeches to promote the theory and rules of improved Chinese bookkeeping. We hereby inform your association and hope that you will notify all members to attend the meeting at that time to participate in and learn from each other.

Ten Features The features of improved Chinese bookkeeping are listed as follows: (1) Each account book is printed with a fixed format, making recording and inspection very convenient. (2) Each account book is printed with registration methods, and accounting can be done in accordance with them. (3) Each account book is printed with accounting instructions, and accounting can have fixed rules. (4) Each account book is printed with a list of managers, and the responsibilities of the accountants are clear. (5) The number of each page is fixed, which can prevent fraud and facilitate inspection. (6) There are many account book programs, and all industries have what they need. (7) The application forms are complete and sufficient for general use. (8) The account book materials are all domestic products, and the printing and binding are both exquisite. (9) The price is low, which can reduce the burden on merchants. (10) There is a service department to serve users at any time.
